<div id="review_724346584" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/724346584" />
    <a title="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei"><img alt="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1421992465p2/2551178.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/724346584?book_show_action=true">Sep 20, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" href="/user/show/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei">Lady Vigilante (Feifei)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/18392290-the-tied-man">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=dark-reads">dark-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=douchenugget">douchenugget</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=oops-let-s-do-it-again-romance">oops-let-s-do-it-again-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=dark-taboo-forbidden-reads">dark-taboo-forbidden-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=i-trust-my-friends">i-trust-my-friends</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=abuse">abuse</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer724346584" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8694127688879406432"><b>2.5 STARS</b><br/><br/>But I am tempted to bump it up to 3.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396557482i/9151885._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I am writing this review with the most peculiar look on my face; the expression is a mix of fascination, befuddlement, annoyance, and complete and utter boredom. <br/><br/><u>
  <b>Fascination:</b>
</u> I’m in awe of Blaine’s character. Yes, you heard me. I think the author has done a brilliant job of portraying an outwardly beautiful, elegant perfectionist but also a diabolical, conniving antagonist. For me, her character intrigued me the most. <br/><br/>The writing is very eloquent </span>
  <span id="freeText8694127688879406432" style="display:none"><b>2.5 STARS</b><br><br>But I am tempted to bump it up to 3.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396557482i/9151885._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I am writing this review with the most peculiar look on my face; the expression is a mix of fascination, befuddlement, annoyance, and complete and utter boredom. <br><br><u>
  <b>Fascination:</b>
</u> I’m in awe of Blaine’s character. Yes, you heard me. I think the author has done a brilliant job of portraying an outwardly beautiful, elegant perfectionist but also a diabolical, conniving antagonist. For me, her character intrigued me the most. <br><br>The writing is very eloquent as well. I don’t think anyone can say that it’s <i>not</i> well-written, because it is.<br><br><u>
  <b>Befuddlement:</b>
</u> Sadly though, the eloquent writing was the major problem I had with the book. It felt too much and I wanted more action, less description. Some things where you just need one sentence to describe took a paragraph. Hence, I was pretty bored for a good 70% of the book. The last 30% captured my attention though, and it explains how I read the last half of the book in a day while it took me 3 days to finish just the first half. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1383149349ra/6416663.gif" width="300" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><u>
  <b>Annoyance:</b>
</u> I really loved the premise of the story and the beginning of the book grabbed my attention but soon after the author lost me with the sometimes too eloquent prose and slang. Then the chapter breaks were infuriating. I’d get a chapter break right between a conversation and it just made NO SENSE to why the characters couldn’t finish their conversation first. Needless to say, it broke my reading flow. <br><br>Also what is with Finn calling Lilith a “stupid cow?” I mean, the first couple of times I’m like okay, it’s an endearment when he’s frustrated but jeez, enough is enough. It's not the cow's fault.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396557482i/9151886.gif" width="300" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><u>
  <b>Boredom:</b>
</u> As for this part, I <u>never</u> connected with any of the characters nor was I invested in the story at all so reading the book felt like I was reading a textbook, vaguely interested but still aloof. I concede that there are a few scenes meant to be disturbing/dark, but for me I felt nothing. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I mean, the heroine was getting her fingers snapped off and poor Finn was stabbed and carved and I didn’t feel a single thing. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1383090583ra/6384270.gif" width="300" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I swear one day, nothing gruesome or heinous I read in books will scare me and that in itself is a scary thought. <br><br>__________________________________________<br><br>I also wrote a mid-book review that has more details. See spoiler.<br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<i>It's taken me 3 days to read half of the book so this is a mid-book review, NOT the full review.</i><br><br>This is spoiler-free.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396464134i/9137488._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="150" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Everyone knows I'm a dark reader. I don't know what exactly about this genre that fascinates me but I know that I'm irrevocably immersed in these reads and can't get enough of them. Naturally, The Tied Man fell under this category and I couldn't wait to start it. <br><br>Except....<i>I didn't.</i><br><br>You know the feeling where you have this book for the longest time, a book that has the stamp of approval from most, if not all, your close reading friends and you get it but there's just <i>something</i> there stopping you from opening it and reading? That kind of feeling? <br><br>Well that's what happened with The Tied Man and I just knew (without even reading the reviews) that I had to be in a certain mood for this book to click with me. It's been almost a year since I've had it and just a couple of days ago, I felt this urge to read it. I felt ready. <br><br>So I started it and this happened:<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396464134i/9137489.jpg" width="300" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I'll admit it...I'm stumped. This is probably the first time I picked up a dark read and can't decide if my feelings are positive/negative. I don't even think I like this book. I mean, for one...the British (I think it's British) slang and dialogue threw me off course so many times I lost count. I put down the book a number of times over the last 3 days yet there's this urge (or OCD lol) that forces me to continue. I like the characters but do I love them? Feel for them? Connect with them? <b>No.</b> There are a few times my heart twinged and felt bad for a certain character but for the most part? <b><i>I don't freaking care.</i></b> <br><br>I don't care about the horses.<br>I don't care about the painting techniques. <br>I don't care what the hall looks like.<br>Strangely enough, I don't care about the history lessons. <br>And I especially don't care for the language. I feel like I'm missing words between the sentences.<br><br>From what I've read so far (around the 51% mark) nothing about the book is dark. Perhaps I hyped it up in my mind too much. And I'm constantly asking myself this question: <i>why am I so emotionally detached from everything?</i> <br><br>I realize there's a load of 5 star ratings but this book is definitely not for everyone and just might not be for me. Nevertheless, I can't find it in myself to DNF it so we shall see about the second half of the story.<br><br><b>To be continued...</b> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="8694127688879406432" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_576484571" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/576484571" />
    <a title="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9080319-allison-will-never-conquer-her-tbr"><img alt="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1465384674p2/9080319.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/576484571?book_show_action=true">Mar 31, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" href="/user/show/9080319-allison-will-never-conquer-her-tbr">Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer576484571" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8594853924148494452"><b>4.5 DARK, GRITTY, TORTUROUS STARS!!<br/><br/>Great debut novel, Tabitha McGowan!!</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/General%20erotic%20stuff/9ebc9c88c26b62539de6e3d3ad935c9a_zpscbb8fee0.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380415628i/820504.jpg' alt=' photo 9ebc9c88c26b62539de6e3d3ad935c9a_zpscbb8fee0.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>I had to sit and digest a bit before coming to a conclusion as to whether I <i>liked</i> this book or not. Then I had to tell myself, my rating isn't exclusively on if I LIKED the story, but how well it was written. Well, the writing was superb. It's written by a British author and in England so I was, once again, marveled at all the British-isms. In fact, a lot of the terms or slang spoken, I had zero clue what they meant. That</span>
  <span id="freeText8594853924148494452" style="display:none"><b>4.5 DARK, GRITTY, TORTUROUS STARS!!<br><br>Great debut novel, Tabitha McGowan!!</b><br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/General%20erotic%20stuff/9ebc9c88c26b62539de6e3d3ad935c9a_zpscbb8fee0.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380415628i/820504.jpg" alt=" photo 9ebc9c88c26b62539de6e3d3ad935c9a_zpscbb8fee0.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I had to sit and digest a bit before coming to a conclusion as to whether I <i>liked</i> this book or not. Then I had to tell myself, my rating isn't exclusively on if I LIKED the story, but how well it was written. Well, the writing was superb. It's written by a British author and in England so I was, once again, marveled at all the British-isms. In fact, a lot of the terms or slang spoken, I had zero clue what they meant. That's always an experience- learning that even though we share a language, the meaning and slang is totally different. <br><br>The story- I really struggle to find an appropriate word for it. On the heels of a very dark read, I am very hesitant to call it simply a dark read. It wasn't necessarily dark as much as UGLY. The villains in this book were straight up monsters. This is what made me struggle to like the story. In fact, there was very little goodness at all. I'm a seasoned reader of those things BDSM, or darker books that bring forth the not so nice side of the human spirit.....this book made me cringe in parts. At the risk of bringing "other books" into a review, my idea of dark or strong BDSM scenes that borderline on a love/hate for me are Dark Duet and Original Sinners (The Prince, specifically). That being said, I still LOVED those books. I think because under all the shit was a fair share of goodness....of love. But this book didn't put much out there for me to grasp as goodness. In fact, one scene about 75% in, I almost stopped the book completely. Let it be known that Tied Man is riddled with non-consensual sex, drug abuse, extreme violence, vulgarity, and everything horrifyingly evil.<br><br>The bulk of the evil comes from Lady Blaine Albermarle. Blaine owns a private retreat on a secluded island in England. She caters to the extreme sexual fantasies of those who can afford such luxury. Unfortunately the scenes are aided by the "use" of Finn, a 24 year old Irish man who is essentially her captive. He's there as a slave and has no chance of escape due to her threats to kill his two sisters in Dublin. She's got direct links to his sisters- one call, they're dead. He won't make it to the mainland. He's tried once, and the failure cost him. The things they did to this man..... (bile enters my throat). I ached for this poor guy. He only survives this life of captivity by living in a prison cell in the cellar and being constantly doped up on drugs. Even though I felt horrible for him, the constant state of drug use and smoking made him a more empathetic character than sexually attractive. <br><br>Finn-<br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Male%20Eye%20Candy/e1f80524c22cc5d2d41e8b4a45ec51d3_zps291014c3.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380415628i/820505.jpg" alt=" photo e1f80524c22cc5d2d41e8b4a45ec51d3_zps291014c3.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Enter Lilith, a famous artist in Spain who is forced to go to the island "retreat" as a payment for her dead-beat dad's lack of payment. She's to paint an erotic picture of the lady of the manor, Blaine. I liked Lilli. She had a spunk to her, an "in your face" nobody controls me attitude. It didn't take long for Blaine to take all that away. When Lilli gets an eyeful of what's done in the manor, and specifically done to Finn, she is devoted to finding a way to protect him. Even if its by entertaining his "clients" for a bit so he isn't brutalized quite so long. But she's got to find a way to get both of them out of there. But with no internet or phones, and being in an island away from all things legal, it makes it difficult. Blaine is a master at using information to blackmail and manipulate everything within her world. <br><br>Lilith-<br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Used%20in%20review/0cb7a462a91a951b3727d254054dd493_zpsc2a6a028.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380415628i/820506._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo 0cb7a462a91a951b3727d254054dd493_zpsc2a6a028.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>So, the reason I didn't rate the book higher is not because of the violence and sheer ugliness of the storyline.... I was just disappointed we didn't get more romantic pull of Finn and Lili together. I know there's feelings there but I think the author could've delved more into "them" as an entity. There was just so much going against them, it would've been nice to get a better baseline as to why they'd do anything to get out of there to be together. Obviously this is not a romance whatsoever. The word love isn't in the book once, I don't believe. They're committed to getting out and the author tells you they want each other, I just didn't FEEL it. <br><br>So go forth...but consider yourself warned. I've never read a more violent, abusive, "ugly" book.......nothing against the actual book, however.... the subject matter was that.</span>
  <a data-text-id="8594853924148494452" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_554149179" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/554149179" />
    <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle"><img alt="Jennifer Kyle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514915429p2/9916227.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/554149179?book_show_action=true">Mar 06, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jennifer Kyle" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle">Jennifer Kyle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9916227-jennifer-kyle?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9916227-jennifer-kyle?shelf=i-like-it-dark-and-twisted">i-like-it-dark-and-twisted</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer554149179" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13742303344577524396"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380412347i/810808.jpg' width='400' height='375' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>4 1/2 Chuisle Stars</b><br/><br/>The Tied Man grabbed my attention from the start of this dark story. I was hooked and although this book came with a WARNING (please read it before starting and take it seriously) there was no turning back for me nor did I want to abandon Finn. My need to know had me reading through some of the toughest scenes I’ve come across in a novel. I found that nothing in this book was erotic nor did I find it very romantic. I did however find it extremely well written.<br/><br/>This story is tol</span>
  <span id="freeText13742303344577524396" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380412347i/810808.jpg" width="400" height="375" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>4 1/2 Chuisle Stars</b><br><br>The Tied Man grabbed my attention from the start of this dark story. I was hooked and although this book came with a WARNING (please read it before starting and take it seriously) there was no turning back for me nor did I want to abandon Finn. My need to know had me reading through some of the toughest scenes I’ve come across in a novel. I found that nothing in this book was erotic nor did I find it very romantic. I did however find it extremely well written.<br><br>This story is told in alternating povs from our artist and the tied man. Lilith Bresson is a world renowned artist who has been coerced into staying at Albermarle Hall. Through a television appearance she captures Finn Strachan ’s eye and Blaine Albermarle uses this to her enjoyment. <br><br><b>
  <i>"Finn had the face of a fallen angel."~Lilith</i>
</b><br><br><b>
  <i>"It was the first time, I ever felt guilt at finding a man attractive."~Lilith</i>
</b><br><br>Lilith has a hell of a past and is stronger than the majority of female heroines I have read. The girl is a survivor and a damn good ally!<br><br>This reader would do anything to save Finn Strachan he is a gorgeous Irish captive and tormented man. (I had devised several plausible plans of rescue and frequently had to remind myself this is just a book.) Finn is trapped and copes with drugs to get through his existence at Albermarle Hall. <br><br><b>
  <i>Y'know what my job is, huh? It's to say 'Yes' and keep saying it until whoever's paying decides they've had enough. It doesn't matter if I'm not happy, or if it disgusts me, or even if it hurts like I'd rather fucking die. So deal with it. I have to."~Finn</i>
</b><br><br>Blaine our ladyship is a sadist who runs this glorified brothel. She has had her claws into Finn for five years and sadly the level of torment she instills on him for her enjoyment escalates. She thrives off his misery and despair. Lilith finds that no one is safe around this MONSTER not even our feisty tough heroine.<br><br>My heart broke repeatedly for Finn and wished that “the plan” would have happened sooner and quicker. This book offered torture to the reader that had me desperately wishing for rainbows and unicorns. <br><br>There are two reasons I gave this book 4 1/2 stars instead of 5 stars: I needed more from Finn and Lilith’s scene in the basement. Possibly 'were in this together' or 'I want a future and I can think in futures', something along those lines. It’s not a cliffhanger but since I went through this hell I wanted an epilogue or some terrific dialogue at the end of this book. Since this didn’t happen, I was left still feeling like the wounds and scars of the torment are still visible and raw. Basically I wanted some sort of declarations...It’s the romantic in me! <br><br>From my stalking efforts of the author’s page, it would appear that there will be a sequel, so this reader will once brave through for Lilith &amp; Finn.<br><br>I want those damn unicorns!!</span>
  <a data-text-id="13742303344577524396" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_718110523" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/718110523" />
    <a title="destini mia" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13742215-destini-mia"><img alt="destini mia" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1499903277p2/13742215.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/718110523?book_show_action=true">Sep 12, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="destini mia" class="user" itemprop="url" name="destini mia" href="/user/show/13742215-destini-mia">destini mia</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13742215-destini-mia?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer718110523" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16655090592153509158"><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>... at the end of the day, everything I do cost me. The only question is how much.</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381878759i/5374487.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>We have Finn...</b><br/><i>
  <blockquote>A nocturnal junkie, scared of needles and scared of the dark. The irony was hilarious.</blockquote>
</i><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381878415ra/5374318.gif' width='500' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Lilith...</b><br/><i>
  <blockquote> "I see what I want to see."</blockquote>
</i><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381880736i/5375658.jpg' width='500' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>And Blaine...</b><br/><i>
  <blockquote> "... his despair arouses her beyond measure."</blockquote>
</i><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381877783ra/5373943.gif' width='500' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Don't even ask me how I survived this book. It will forever remain a mystery. I'm still sitting in shock at the events that have unfolded in <i>The Tied Man</i>. Let me tell you, this takes the cake for <i>d</i></span>
  <span id="freeText16655090592153509158" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>... at the end of the day, everything I do cost me. The only question is how much.</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381878759i/5374487.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>We have Finn...</b><br><i>
  <blockquote>A nocturnal junkie, scared of needles and scared of the dark. The irony was hilarious.</blockquote>
</i><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381878415ra/5374318.gif" width="500" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Lilith...</b><br><i>
  <blockquote> "I see what I want to see."</blockquote>
</i><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381880736i/5375658.jpg" width="500" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>And Blaine...</b><br><i>
  <blockquote> "... his despair arouses her beyond measure."</blockquote>
</i><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381877783ra/5373943.gif" width="500" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Don't even ask me how I survived this book. It will forever remain a mystery. I'm still sitting in shock at the events that have unfolded in <i>The Tied Man</i>. Let me tell you, this takes the cake for <i>dark &amp; disturbing reads</i>. It makes everything else I've ever read seem like child's play... something I'd find in the Children's Literature section in Barnes &amp; Nobles right next to Harry Potter. <br><br>Lilith is practically forced to go to Albermarle Hall to settle a debt her good-for-nothing father has put her in. As a highly accomplished artist, she's expected to paint a portrait of Lady Albermarle and leave society behind, reluctantly relinquishing all her electronic devices. <br>Stuck on the island for months, Lilith's only end goal is to get the hell out of there as soon as possible. <br>However, a simple proposition changes <i>everything</i>.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381543220i/5006928._SY540_.jpg" width="500" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Where to even begin? <br>I almost felt guilty for loving this books so much. The actions that take place, the manipulation... it was <b>horrible.</b> And I mean, carry a spare barf bag in my purse just in case something became too much. And yet, I couldn't tear my eyes away. The complex characters, the story... I completely immersed myself in <i>The Tied Man.</i><br><br>Lilith was one of those characters that, in real life, you'd either love her or hate her. She was a bit hard and definitely lacked a serious filter. But as I kept reading, she really grew on me. She's someone that you'd know whatever came out of her mouth was 100% bullshit free. I would even get excited to see what would fall out of her mouth next. <br><br><b>Lilith</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381880736i/5375659._SY540_.jpg" width="500" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>My poor, beautiful boy Finn... ♥ <br>How my heart broke for him. You haven't experienced all consuming, soul-crushing pain for a character until you've read this book. You just gravitate towards Finn. He is the true meaning of <i>bent but not broken.</i> I can say with all honestly that I would not have been as strong as him. The things he's experienced... it went beyond cruel. And he still fought back, in his own small ways. <br><br><b>Finn</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381881301i/5376033._SY540_.png" width="500" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>If you could add up all my adoration, admiration, and respect for Finn and turn it into hatred... that would just scratch the <i>surface</i> of my feelings for Blaine. What a inhuman character. She made me want to just bash my head in. If she would just scream, rage, or just crack her façade for a second, <b>maybe</b> I wouldn't despise her as much as I do now but there wasn't a slip up, not a single thing that could, at least, make me feel good for a second. She was like a cold robot, that no matter what you did, she would take it all in stride and come up with something ten times worse. <br><i>
  <blockquote> In my long and illustrious career I had been fucked by a procession of evil bastards, but none ever quite matched the sublime cruelty of Blaine.</blockquote>
</i><br><br><b>Blaine</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381881792i/5376207._SY540_.png" width="500" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Lilith and Finn's relationship was a slow burn and I wouldn't have wanted it any other way. It made things <b>real.</b> Like it wasn't another fuck to them. They had a foundation of friendship and trust and seeing them grow, together and on their own, was beautiful. <br><i>
  <blockquote> "You're the first person in this whole fucking place who's ever asked permission to touch me, you know that?"</blockquote>
</i><br>In the beginning, the writing took a bit of getting used to. It was British and Tabitha didn't spell everything out for you. I would find things flying completely over my head. Once you get the hang of it, though, it was seamless. I <b>loved</b> it. Nothing was handed to you on a platter and it enhanced the complexity of the story and characters. <br><br>I'm not going to lie and say this books if for everybody, because it's <b>not.</b> But if you can stomach it, <i>The Tied Man</i> is a heartbreaking, absolute <b>must read.</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381884136i/5377362.jpg" width="500" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="16655090592153509158" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_610628017" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/610628017" />
    <a title="☆ Sammy ☆彡" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14144676-sammy"><img alt="☆ Sammy ☆彡" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1462053159p2/14144676.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/610628017?book_show_action=true">May 08, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="☆ Sammy ☆彡" class="user" itemprop="url" name="☆ Sammy ☆彡" href="/user/show/14144676-sammy">☆ Sammy ☆彡</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14144676-sammy?shelf=dark-and-twisted">dark-and-twisted</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14144676-sammy?shelf=emotionally-intense">emotionally-intense</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer610628017" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4746430238733846620">For me, reading The Tied Man was like taking a tumble down the rabbit hole and ending up in a very intense, dark, & twisted place that is controlled by an evil bitch. <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380420882ra/835468.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Before you consider reading this book, you really need to heed the author's warning: <b>Please note that this storyline contains depictions of drug abuse, violence and non-consensual sexual activity.</b> <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379798703i/644318.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>If you have any issues with these topics, this may not be the book for you.</b><br/><br/>Lilith Bresson is a strong, independent, and successful artis</span>
  <span id="freeText4746430238733846620" style="display:none">For me, reading The Tied Man was like taking a tumble down the rabbit hole and ending up in a very intense, dark, &amp; twisted place that is controlled by an evil bitch. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380420882ra/835468.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Before you consider reading this book, you really need to heed the author's warning: <b>Please note that this storyline contains depictions of drug abuse, violence and non-consensual sexual activity.</b> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379798703i/644318.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>If you have any issues with these topics, this may not be the book for you.</b><br><br>Lilith Bresson is a strong, independent, and successful artist who values having control over her life. Her control, however, is tested when her father forces her to repay one of his debts by painting the portrait of Lady Blaine Albermarle. In order to complete this project, Lilith must stay at Albermarle Hall, an island estate that Blaine owns where electronic devices such as computers, phones, MP3 players, etc. are not allowed. During her stay at Albermarle Hall, Lilith learns about the horrific business being conducted on the estate and that Blaine is not the woman that she appears to be. She also meets Blaine's "companion", Finn, who is a quiet, disturbed, and very unhappy man.<br><br>I felt a whirlwind of emotions while reading this book: anger, disgust, sadness, hopelessness, a little happy, and a lot of hatred toward the villain. <br><br>I think the hardest part of this book for me was Finn's situation. His story ripped my heart out and I just wanted to whisk him away and protect him from all the horrors he had to live through.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/558750.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Finn: <br><blockquote>
  <i>"I want to keep hold of just one or two poxy secrets in the car crash otherwise known as my life in vain hope that once or twice a year I can pretend to have some bloody dignity."</i>
</blockquote><br><br>Finn to Lilith: <br><blockquote>
  <i>"You came back," he whispered. "You did all that, and you still came back."</i>
</blockquote><br><br>Overall, I would give this book <b>5 dark &amp; emotional stars</b>. If you think that you can handle what the author mentioned in her warning, then I encourage you to read this book. <br><br>I am looking forward to seeing Finn &amp; Lili's story continued in the second book. I did feel that the ending of the Tied Man was a little abrupt, but I can understand the author's view that an epilogue really wouldn't do this story justice. Finn and Lili both have a lot of healing to do and demons to overcome. </span>
  <a data-text-id="4746430238733846620" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2190064-nenia-socially-awkward-trash-panda-campbell?shelf=kindle-unlimited">kindle-unlimited</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2190064-nenia-socially-awkward-trash-panda-campbell?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2330791722" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8624262126594995154"><a href='http://readasaurus.blogspot.com/' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1459070464i/18565492.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><a href='https://www.instagram.com/curvybeefashions/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Instagram</a> || <a href='https://twitter.com/NeniaCampbell' rel='nofollow noopener'>Twitter</a> || <a href='https://www.facebook.com/aficionenias/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Facebook</a> || <a href='http://www.amazon.com/Nenia-Campbell/e/B00AWVRKMS' rel='nofollow noopener'>Amazon</a> || <a href='https://www.pinterest.com/mightbeamisprin/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Pinterest</a><br/><br/><br/>THE TIED MAN is a book that's been on my radar for years, but I never got around to reading it myself until <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3081072447' rel='nofollow noopener'>Heather</a> invited me to buddy read it with her via Kindle Unlimited. The premise is pretty interesting, even though it seems like standard new adult fare at a glance: beautiful and sexually autonomous heroine, Lilith, is a professional erotic artist who ends up being invited to an exclusive and prestigious estate to do a commission t</span>
  <span id="freeText8624262126594995154" style="display:none"><a href="http://readasaurus.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1459070464i/18565492.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="https://www.instagram.com/curvybeefashions/" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> || <a href="https://twitter.com/NeniaCampbell" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> || <a href="https://www.facebook.com/aficionenias/" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a> || <a href="http://www.amazon.com/Nenia-Campbell/e/B00AWVRKMS" rel="nofollow noopener">Amazon</a> || <a href="https://www.pinterest.com/mightbeamisprin/" rel="nofollow noopener">Pinterest</a><br><br><br>THE TIED MAN is a book that's been on my radar for years, but I never got around to reading it myself until <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3081072447" rel="nofollow noopener">Heather</a> invited me to buddy read it with her via Kindle Unlimited. The premise is pretty interesting, even though it seems like standard new adult fare at a glance: beautiful and sexually autonomous heroine, Lilith, is a professional erotic artist who ends up being invited to an exclusive and prestigious estate to do a commission to the reclusive lady, Blaine, whom her philandering father owes a debt. Once there, she sees the most beautiful man she's ever laid eyes on in her life: a young Irish man named Finn, Blaine's personal companion.<br><br><br><br>Lilith has a knack for reading people, though, and despite her initial attraction to Finn, she realizes that something about his situation isn't quite right. He doesn't seem to <i>want </i>to be there-- and then, she realizes to her horror that not only does he not want to be there, he also can't ever leave. That's when she learns about the true horrors hiding in the gilded shadows of the estate-- dark, twisted horrors of humanity at its lowest-- and if she's not careful, she'll also become sucked into the twisted machinations of Blaine, too.<br><br><br><br>This is honestly one of the best books I've read in a while. It packs an emotionally devastating wallop, made all the more effective by my investment in the characters. It's got trigger warnings all across the board, so it's definitely not one for the faint-hearted. I don't think I've seen a male character go through this much torture since Jude from <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2675835006" rel="nofollow noopener">A LITTLE LIFE</a>, or Jamie from <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2112087707" rel="nofollow noopener">OUTLANDER</a>. And the villain is the absolute <i>worst</i>-- I haven't seen such innovative displays of sociopathy since reading and being scarred for life by <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1999567358" rel="nofollow noopener">THE LAST INNOCENT HOUR</a>.<br><br><br><br>Part of what makes this book halfway tolerable on an emotional level is the tenderness between Lilith and Finn. Their relationship is slow-burn, as it should be, and one of the most touching scenes in this book is when Finn lets down his guard around her completely and she is so sweet and patient with him, it just about broke my heart. THE TIED MAN did such a great job showing how intimacy and sex are not necessarily mutually inclusive, and how difficult it can be to overcome abuse.<br><br><br><br>I actually didn't like Lilith much at all in the beginning because she felt so artificial, but her character grew on me and by the end, I actually quite admired her strength. In the author's profile, she said that she was inspired to create a heroine in a dark story who wasn't just a foil for the hero, and I think she succeeded. The damsel saves the hero in this one, and it's really, really exciting to read a book that does that so well, even as it plunges to depths where most writers normally don't dare to tread.<br><br><br><br>This was really excellent. I hope the author writes more books someday. She's exceptionally talented.<br><br><br><br>4.5 stars</span>

<div id="review_515933864" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/515933864" />
    <a title="A. Bookzilla." class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/266923-a-bookzilla"><img alt="A. Bookzilla." src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1372196458p2/266923.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/515933864?book_show_action=true">Jan 24, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="A. Bookzilla." class="user" itemprop="url" name="A. Bookzilla." href="/user/show/266923-a-bookzilla">A. Bookzilla.</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/266923-a-bookzilla?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/266923-a-bookzilla?shelf=2013-absolute-favorites">2013-absolute-favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/266923-a-bookzilla?shelf=will-re-read">will-re-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/266923-a-bookzilla?shelf=want-own-in-print">want-own-in-print</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/266923-a-bookzilla?shelf=really-dark">really-dark</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/266923-a-bookzilla?shelf=cbl-guest-review">cbl-guest-review</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/266923-a-bookzilla?shelf=dare-me">dare-me</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/266923-a-bookzilla?shelf=books-with-a-finn">books-with-a-finn</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer515933864" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11989581947385857113">Well, that was one hell of a ride. But before I write this out, a fair warning - because I wish I had been warned beforehand.<br/><br/><i>
  <b>This book is most definitely not for the faint of heart. It portrays some really sick sexual behaviour, non-consensual sex, heavy drug abuse and extreme violence. Mature audience only - I can't stress this enough.</b>
</i><br/><br/>And to think my worst fear was that this was a historical romance of some sort (It's not! It's a contemporary.) I just wasn't prepared for this.<br/><br/>I loved the bo</span>
  <span id="freeText11989581947385857113" style="display:none">Well, that was one hell of a ride. But before I write this out, a fair warning - because I wish I had been warned beforehand.<br /><br /><i>
  <b>This book is most definitely not for the faint of heart. It portrays some really sick sexual behaviour, non-consensual sex, heavy drug abuse and extreme violence. Mature audience only - I can't stress this enough.</b>
</i><br /><br />And to think my worst fear was that this was a historical romance of some sort (It's not! It's a contemporary.) I just wasn't prepared for this.<br /><br />I loved the book. The author really has a way with words, I could almost see the prison that is Albermarle Hall, the characters are so alive they seem like real people. The horror of the story was unspeakable, and yet, she managed to weave one of the sweetest love stories into it. I don't remember the last time I was rooting for the protagonists or cared about them so much.<br /><br />The story is pretty simple - the wicked witch is holding the prince captive in her castle, and the princess has to save him.<br /><br />Lilith is this extremely strong, intelligent and absolutely unbreakable spirit. Even if at the beginning her attitude was putting me off, I just knew I'd rather be on her side than the opposite.<br /><br />Finn, the sweet, sweet man. Everyone has failed him. I just wanted to hug him and keep all the harm away from him. Now there's a character that, even completely emasculated, was the strongest I've ever read. I just felt for him so much.<br /><br />God, I hated the vicious game Blaine was playing with the two of them. Despite how intense the story is, the budding romance is so subtle, there's a really slow build-up between the two of them and for some strange reason, it completely worked - it's a nice contrast to all the intense things that were happening, peaceful and sweet. There's great chemistry between Finn and Lilith, but it only takes center stage every once in a while.<br /><br />Every time the violence and the abuse would happen, I kept thinking it just couldn't get any worse than it was at that moment, dreading every next scene, but I couldn't make myself put it down! I sobbed during a particularly bad scene, I just hoped that was the worst the author would throw our way. <br /><br />There are some really suspenseful moments that keep you on the edge of the seat, but there was also some comic relief that had me laugh out loud. The horror moments were exactly that, horror. I have no doubt in my mind that something like this is happening somewhere and that only adds to how horrific it all feels. Human beings are capable of this.<br />But seriously, the writing was terrific! Such colorful characters, great development, so many layers to each of them. THE DIALOGUE! Absolutely amazing.<br /><br />After that warning, I don't even have to say there are some graphic sex and violence scenes in this. Most of it isn't hot by a long shot, so don't expect that. It's just plain disturbing, and painfully detailed.<br />On the other hand, the sex between the main characters was...sweet, in a word.<br /><br />I wasn't satisfied with the ending, I needed just a tad more than that. Don't worry, everything is tied up nicely in the end, I just needed some more Finn and Lilith. However, the sequel is being written as you are reading this, so no doubt, we'll see more of Tabitha's beautiful writing and Finn and Lilith's story.<br /><br />This review is long enough, but no doubt I'll think of more to say later. Do I recommend it? If you're into this genre, <b>I most definitely do</b>. This automatically went to the top of my 2013 favorites shelf.<br /><br />I am proud to be a guest reviewer at <a href="http://www.cblreviews.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">❤ Coffee, Books &amp; Lipgloss Book Review Blog ❤</a>!</span>
  <a data-text-id="11989581947385857113" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer831727187" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer11127287148878931469"><br/><b>THE TIED MAN</b> is a dark fairy tale where the Princess comes to save the Prince.<br/><br/>♦<b>Lilith</b>♦ is the princess in this twisted tale. <br/><br/>♦<b>Finn</b>♦ is the "Rapunzel" of Albermarle Hall.<br/><br/>♦<b>Blaine</b>♦ is the evil queen. <br/><br/>The Tied Man is kind of like the 'boy' version of <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12513614.Captive_in_the_Dark__The_Dark_Duet___1_' title='Captive in the Dark (The Dark Duet, #1) by C.J. Roberts' rel='nofollow noopener'>Captive in the Dark</a> and <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17615896.Escape_from_Paradise__Paradise___1_' title='Escape from Paradise (Paradise, #1) by Gwendolyn Field' rel='nofollow noopener'>Escape from Paradise</a>.<br/><br/>My only issue I found with the story is the foreign lingo because it kept tripping me up. The writing style made it hard for me to be fully immersed in the story because it took awhile to get use to it. Other</span>
  <span id="freeText11127287148878931469" style="display:none"><br><b>THE TIED MAN</b> is a dark fairy tale where the Princess comes to save the Prince.<br><br>♦<b>Lilith</b>♦ is the princess in this twisted tale. <br><br>♦<b>Finn</b>♦ is the "Rapunzel" of Albermarle Hall.<br><br>♦<b>Blaine</b>♦ is the evil queen. <br><br>The Tied Man is kind of like the 'boy' version of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12513614.Captive_in_the_Dark__The_Dark_Duet___1_" title="Captive in the Dark (The Dark Duet, #1) by C.J. Roberts" rel="nofollow noopener">Captive in the Dark</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17615896.Escape_from_Paradise__Paradise___1_" title="Escape from Paradise (Paradise, #1) by Gwendolyn Field" rel="nofollow noopener">Escape from Paradise</a>.<br><br>My only issue I found with the story is the foreign lingo because it kept tripping me up. The writing style made it hard for me to be fully immersed in the story because it took awhile to get use to it. Otherwise it was a good dark and twisted tale. <br><br><b>SERIES:</b><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17237477.The_Tied_Man__The_Tied_Man___1_" title="The Tied Man (The Tied Man, #1) by Tabitha McGowan" rel="nofollow noopener">

  <span id="freeText13994193526502617116" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401972i/780787._SX540_.jpg" width="125" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>♥♥♥ 5 'Destroyed Me' Stars ♥♥♥</b><br><br><br><blockquote>

  </b>
</blockquote><br>I have no idea how to review this book. No bloody idea. This might end up being quite brief because I just don't know what to say. A lot of it might be repetetive, so sorry in advance, but my brain just can't function at the moment. All I know is, the writing was brilliant.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg" width="405" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380419127i/830589._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>“I don't expect you to be like them. Don't want you to be. It's not them I want, it's you. From the moment we met, it's only been you.” <br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><b>Lilith Bresson</b> is a renowned independent artist who lives in Spain. One day her piece of shite father, asks Lili to help him pay a debt to Lady Blaine Albermarle. She initially refuses but after her father threatens to get a restraining order to keep her from her much younger sibling, she relents. She then agrees to paint a portrait to pay the debt. Little did she know that in doing so, she would end up in hell. I loved how freaking blunt Lili was. She was herself and no one else, and of course she made no apologies for it. She was feisty and funny in a sarcastic way. She was strong and witty. I thought she was the perfect person to challenge the Mega bitch that is Blaine Albermarle. As well as the perfect person to show Finn what love is and how it feels to have someone care. I loved this character and getting to be in her mind.<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380419127i/830590._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>“What did you call me?”<br><br>“Ah. A chuisle. Gaelic. 'My darling'. I prefer the proper translation, mind you.”<br><br>“Which is?”<br><br>He gave a bashful smile. “My pulse.”<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Oh my poor beautiful <b>Finn Strachan</b>. How I wanted to hug him and kiss him and make it all better for him. I wanted to desperately help him escape the nightmare he was living. Finn was an Irish man that fell into the hands of Blaine Albermarle and became her "companion". What he really was, was a play thing, sex toy to be used in whatever manner you wished to use him. Even if that meant causing him bodily harm. My heart hurt so DEEPLY for him. I cried at what was done to him. I became ANGRY at those who inflicted pain upon him. It teared me up completely. My heart was chewed up piece by piece and spit out. That's how much I hurt for this beautifully wonderful man. A lot of it was quite graphic, so be aware that this is most definitely not for everyone.<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380419127i/830591._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>“Lili- no ones ever done anything like this for me. Ever. Are you hearing me? I sure as hell know I wouldn’t have taken the risks you did today just for a whore.”<br><br>“Don’t say that.”<br><br>“It’s what I am.”<br><br>“It’s what she makes you do. It’s not who you are.”<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Then there was the super MONSTER heartless bitch from hell, <b>Blaine Albermarle</b>. Oh, how I friggin' LOATHED her!! I'm not sure I've ever hated a character more. She was a sick sadistic twat. I seriously don't know what to say... HATE just doesn't seem enough. The things she let happen, the lies, the blackmailing, ARGH!! I get pissed off just thinking about it. I wanted a terrible end for this crazy witch, and even though I didn't get to see it, I hope she suffers for it all. Throughout the book, I was plotting bad things for this character. I am not a violent person, mind you (yeah, I know you can totally tell by this review, huh?) but she brought out the worst in me. I wanted to kill her and save my poor Finn and Henry. And that's all I'm going to say about her. BITCH!<br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380419127ra/830592.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b><i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>“I can’t do this alone, Finn. I need you beside me.”</i><br><br>Nobody had ever said that to me.<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br>This book has scarred me. I will never forget it. It terrifies me completely that I know stuff like this actually exists and it SICKENS me. I repeatedly kept asking myself why I chose to put myself through this and to just stop reading the damn book. But the thing is... I couldn't. As much as I wanted to, Finn and Lilith would not let me. I had to know what would become of them. From the moment I read the first page, I was hooked. I was shocked, hurt, angry, felt love, sorrow, and laughter. This book brought a wide range of emotions from me. That's what the writing did to me, it was that amazing. Yes, the story contained some HIDEOUS AND HORRIBLE content, but still the book was great. If I had to complain about anything in the book, it would probably be the ending. Not because it sucked, because in truth, it was beautiful and I LOVED that it wasn't overtly sweet. I mean it just wouldn't have felt real. But it did leave me wanting more. So, I would have liked an epilogue or something. Otherwise, a fantastic read.<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg" width="405" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>
  <i>Please note that this storyline contains depictions of drug abuse, violence and non-consensual sexual activity. This may not be suitable for everyone.</i>
</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="13994193526502617116" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_617812990" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/617812990" />
    <a title="Jennifer" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4482512-jennifer"><img alt="Jennifer" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1374781588p2/4482512.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/617812990?book_show_action=true">May 17, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jennifer" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jennifer" href="/user/show/4482512-jennifer">Jennifer</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4482512-jennifer?shelf=mindfuck">mindfuck</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4482512-jennifer?shelf=tears-sniff">tears-sniff</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer617812990" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10163965154799570415"><b>4 EVIL STARS!!!!!</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>The whole bloody world, populated by monsters.</i>
</b><br/><br/>This is the hardest book I’ve ever read. I have a really dark place inside my brain, and I’ve read some dark twisted stuff, but this takes the cake. You know those dark books that give you a little hope to hold onto? This is not one of those books. <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380421936ra/838867.gif' alt='' width='500px' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img alt='' width='500' height='256' src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380421936ra/838868.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img alt='' width='500' height='230' src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380421936ra/838869.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This book highlights the worst of humanity. <b>Who do you become when you think no one’s watching?</b><br/><br/>The story is set on an island resort. The resort provides your every wish, your every dre</span>
  <span id="freeText10163965154799570415" style="display:none"><b>4 EVIL STARS!!!!!</b><br><br><b>
  <i>The whole bloody world, populated by monsters.</i>
</b><br><br>This is the hardest book I’ve ever read. I have a really dark place inside my brain, and I’ve read some dark twisted stuff, but this takes the cake. You know those dark books that give you a little hope to hold onto? This is not one of those books. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380421936ra/838867.gif" alt="" width="500px" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img alt="" width="500" height="256" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380421936ra/838868.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img alt="" width="500" height="230" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380421936ra/838869.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book highlights the worst of humanity. <b>Who do you become when you think no one’s watching?</b><br><br>The story is set on an island resort. The resort provides your every wish, your every dream, your deepest darkest secret desires. Only the wealthiest can afford to pay for their deepest desires.<br> <br>Finn is on staff at this resort, and he is trapped. No, trapped isn’t enough. He is <b>tortured.</b> He is almost a ghost of a person. Finn lives the most <b>agonizing</b> life that you can imagine. I wanted Finn to die, to kill himself, only to give him one ounce of peace.<br><br><b>My Finn:</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421936i/838870.jpg" alt="." class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>It was easy to forget that other people lived in a world where rules and laws and common sense could keep you safe. A world where, if you did the right thing you were allowed to get on with your life in whichever way you chose.</i>
</b><br><br>Lilith Bresson begins as a strong feminine, fucking hilarious character. She is a famous painter. Throughout the book, she is slowly broken, even more so than when she started. She is manipulated by the resort owner (satan incarnate) to come to the resort, only to be blackmailed into staying and doing the owner’s bidding, painting when and what the owner decides.<br><br><b>
  <i>The summer I met Lilith Bresson, I had begun to die.</i>
</b><br><br><b>My Lilith:</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421936i/838871._SY540_.jpg" alt="Olivia wilde" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I wouldn’t call this a love story. I would call this a survival story. These two characters come together to survive. <br><br><b>Additional Thoughts:</b><br><br><b>Power.</b> I hate power. I wish I could grab it by the bullocks and squeeze until it explodes and ceases to exist. No one could ever have power over another person ever again!!!<br><br><b>Pride.</b> It’s the first sin. It’s the ugliest of sins. It makes us believe we are better...better than another human being. <br><br><b>Manipulation.</b> It is the weakness of the weak, the insecure, the unintelligent….the evil.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380394835i/760328._SX540_.jpg" alt="à la Mode St. » fashion" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book makes me want to stand up for every single person who was ever <b>bullied, abused, beaten, neglected, or never loved</b>.<br> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380394835i/760328._SX540_.jpg" alt="à la Mode St. » fashion" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I will never look at <b>teddy bears</b> the same. They will forever be a <b>
  <i>pathetic pile of overpriced fake fur and anthropomorphic bullshit.</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380394835i/760328._SX540_.jpg" alt="à la Mode St. » fashion" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Why did I give this book 4 stars?</b><br><br>1. I am a <b>
  <i> serial escapologist.</i>
</b> but I couldn’t escape. I want books that allow me to escape. I don’t want to face the reality and horrors of humanity. But I didn’t have a choice with this book. <br><br>2. Yes, Tabitha McGowan is a great writer, but I’ve read better, so I just couldn’t give her that last star.<br><br>3. It feels wrong to celebrate this book. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421936i/838872._SY540_.jpg" alt="4318_original.jpg (834×958)" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>Eat, drink, and be merry, for tomorrow we die.</i>
</b><br></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer15844799833342508510">If you can't handle sick and twisted, this book probably isn't for you.<br/><br/>If you love a total <b> EMOTIONAL </b>.....<br/><a href='http://s1341.photobucket.com/user/shannon_phillips6/media/rollercoaster_zps1ee431ab.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

Lilith is my favorite type of heroine; strong, smart, independent and she has a hilariously smart mouth. She is able to see Finn in a way no one else can and she's able to see more in him than he can see in himself.<br/><br/>Ah, Finn...poor Finn doesn't <i>"live in a world where rules and laws and common se</i></span>
  <span id="freeText15844799833342508510" style="display:none">If you can't handle sick and twisted, this book probably isn't for you.<br><br>If you love a total <b> EMOTIONAL </b>.....<br><a href="http://s1341.photobucket.com/user/shannon_phillips6/media/rollercoaster_zps1ee431ab.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/597623.gif" alt=" photo rollercoaster_zps1ee431ab.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>you'll probably love this book!<br><br>I loved Lilith and Finn as much as I have any characters ever. Lilith is my favorite type of heroine; strong, smart, independent and she has a hilariously smart mouth. She is able to see Finn in a way no one else can and she's able to see more in him than he can see in himself.<br><br>Ah, Finn...poor Finn doesn't <i>"live in a world where rules and laws and common sense could keep you safe. A world where, if you did the right thing you where allowed to get on with your life in whichever way you choose"</i> Finn lives in <b>HELL!</b> A hell where <i>at the end of the day everything cost him. The only question was how much" </i> There is something so angelic about him it was almost impossible for me to endure his ordeal. <br><br>This is such a gut wrenching story of perseverance over the harshest of circumstances. Circumstances, where the victims were thrust because they put others first. I think we all have people or things in our life in which we would be willing to endure anything. It asks the question <i>"Do you think everyone has a price"</i></span>

<div id="review_543406448" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/543406448" />
    <a title="Vikki ~ *squee* lite ~" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3758447-vikki-squee-lite"><img alt="Vikki ~ *squee* lite ~" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1368215503p2/3758447.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/543406448?book_show_action=true">Feb 22, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Vikki ~ *squee* lite ~" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Vikki ~ *squee* lite ~" href="/user/show/3758447-vikki-squee-lite">Vikki ~ *squee* lite ~</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3758447-vikki-squee-lite?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3758447-vikki-squee-lite?shelf=serious-issues">serious-issues</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3758447-vikki-squee-lite?shelf=made-me-want-to-stab-fictional-peop">made-me-want-to-stab-fictional-peop</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3758447-vikki-squee-lite?shelf=didn-t-think-i-would-make-it-out">didn-t-think-i-would-make-it-out</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3758447-vikki-squee-lite?shelf=dark-and-twisted">dark-and-twisted</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer543406448" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9556385067718010020"><br/><br/> <br/><a href='http://s50.beta.photobucket.com/user/vikkimathews/media/4fd3b1b8a4d921f9d64e1c2d59e49602_zps5b0c719b.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410762i/805914.jpg' alt=' photo 4fd3b1b8a4d921f9d64e1c2d59e49602_zps5b0c719b.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><br/>I just have to say, this book had me hooked from the beginning. The writing itself is far better than most of the books that I’ve picked up recently, it’s smart without becoming unrelatable. The dialogue is fantastic, and the descriptions are just enough paint the picture without bogging you down in extraneous details. There is a hunting, “creepy” quality to the book, and I’m not totally sure exactly how the author pulled off, but it was there, in every page.<br/><br/>This isn’t “dark erotica” – ther</span>
  <span id="freeText9556385067718010020" style="display:none"><br><br> <br><a href="http://s50.beta.photobucket.com/user/vikkimathews/media/4fd3b1b8a4d921f9d64e1c2d59e49602_zps5b0c719b.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410762i/805914.jpg" alt=" photo 4fd3b1b8a4d921f9d64e1c2d59e49602_zps5b0c719b.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>I just have to say, this book had me hooked from the beginning. The writing itself is far better than most of the books that I’ve picked up recently, it’s smart without becoming unrelatable. The dialogue is fantastic, and the descriptions are just enough paint the picture without bogging you down in extraneous details. There is a hunting, “creepy” quality to the book, and I’m not totally sure exactly how the author pulled off, but it was there, in every page.<br><br>This isn’t “dark erotica” – there is nothing erotic about most of what happens in the book, and I wouldn’t classify it as a romance either, at least not in a traditional sense.<br><br>To me, it was very much the classic story of good versus evil. It was the story of two people, cut off from the world and real human connection, one self-imposed, one trapped by a bad decision, who find salvation in connection to each other. <br><br>Lilith is a survivor. She has survived a horrible childhood, which has taught her she cannot rely on anyone but herself. She has learned not to make connections with anyone. She has people in her life, but they are kept at a careful distance. She is a famous artist, whose unique talent lies in being able to capture the people behind the façade. She has almost psychic like ability to read people, and put together small details to uncover the secrets they try to hide.<br><br>Finn is survivor. He is trapped in a horrific situation that he cannot escape from. He has endured treatment that honestly, made me sick to my stomach more than once. He has given up the idea that there will ever be salvation, and is slowly slipping away. That is, until he sees Lilli.<br><br>From the moment they meet, there is a connection. One they both try to fight for their own reasons. Together they survive Blaine, who is frankly the most evil character I have ever come across. Neither of them wants to need each other. Neither of them believes that there can be a happy ending. But they find strength in each other, in their connection, in knowing that there is another human being who would sacrifice themselves for them, and they <b>take </b> their happy ending.<br><br>I adored Finn and Lilli like I haven’t adored a couple in a long time. They were so beautiful, so flawed, and so perfect for each other. I’m not sure there was anyone else in the world who could have made Lilli care, or anyone else who could have seen beyond all of Finns past enough to see the real man beneath all the tragedy.<br><br>There is so much about this story that is horrific, but it is still punctuated with these moments of humor, of friendship, of connection, that keep it from just being to hard to take. <br>It is highly recommended. My last warning though….<br><br><a href="http://s50.beta.photobucket.com/user/vikkimathews/media/2101eb176771a7bfc2e1136878ff692d_zpsb36027ea.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410762i/805915.jpg" alt=" photo 2101eb176771a7bfc2e1136878ff692d_zpsb36027ea.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> <br><br>*********************<br>Shit. That was... I don't even know what to say... Horrible and amazing all in one. Full review to come later, after I don't feel like vomiting while simultaneously doing a victory dance. </span>
  <a data-text-id="9556385067718010020" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>
